See ya 'round.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">没事的。我们会找到元凶完美解决异变的，再见~</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_1-47" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 1&quot;,47&#93;"><td id="雪村布返" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雪村布返</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Later!</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">再见！</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-status-header" id="Stage_1-48" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 1&quot;,48&#93;"><td class="tt-s" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td colspan="2" class="tt-status" lang="zh"><div class="poem"><a href="./雪村布返.md" title="雪村布返">雪村布返</a> 退场</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_1-49" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 1&quot;,49&#93;"><td id="风见幽香" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">风见幽香</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">You seem uncharacteristicallyaltruistic today, Marisa. Ya think someone else could copy my style of danmaku?</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">怎么可能？我当然是真货啦。有谁能模仿我弹幕的风格呢？</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_1-52" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 1&quot;,52&#93;"><td id="风见幽香" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">风见幽香</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">I mean, you did copymy giant laser beams...</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">你好好想想你的魔炮是怎么来的吧…<br><br></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

## Stage 3
[](./文件-东方实在相st3.png.md)  [](./文件-东方实在相st3.png.md)3面场景

But now, we can make you under stand that<br>You didn’t need to do it.<br>This is the story of a girl who was not content to take the incongruity of existence lying down.<br>Hearts will never be broken again.<br>My thoughts will follow you into your dreams.<br></div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">曾经爱过但又失去会比不置爱过要好吗?<br>荒谬至极，吾情愿从未对君动心。<br><br>君之愿，依然是想浪费别人的时间吗?<br>抑或是让曾经爱过君的人后悔不已?<br><br>我之憧憬，我之愿望，<br>游遍幻想乡至尽头，向世界展示我之挚爱。<br><br>我不能自已，我情不自禁，<br>唯有划破我之存在界限，以命相抵。<br><br>我愤怒却无处宣世，<br>于境遇，于世界，于存在自身。<br><br>若我修此相之树如愿以偿，<br>若此相之树修世界如愿以偿。<br><br>君本应悔恨伤我之心，<br>现如今只需丢弃，因为没有意义。<br><br>这是一个女孩的心路历程，<br>她不满足于放下不和谐的存在。<br><br>至此，心灵不会再受到伤害。<br>我之思绪将随君消敬于君之梦中。<br></div></td></tr><tr class="tt-status-header" id="Stage_6-219" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 6&quot;,219&#93;"><td class="tt-s" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td colspan="2" class="tt-status" lang="zh"><div class="poem"><a href="./灯笼坂爱美.md" title="灯笼坂爱美">灯笼坂爱美</a> 复活</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_6-220" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 6&quot;,220&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">灯笼坂爱美</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Did you think it wouldn't occur tous to modify the spell card rules?</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">难道你们就没有想过，我们没有考虑过修改符卡规则吗？<br></div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_6-221" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 6&quot;,221&#93;"><td id="鬼人正邪" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">鬼人正邪</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">...!!!</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">……！！！</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_6-222" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 6&quot;,222&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">灯笼坂爱美</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Well, they're mostly thesame. ## Ending No. 02

- <font color="Red"> **剧透提示:  *以下内容包含详细故事情节，请自行决定是否继续阅读* ** </font>


<table><tbody><tr class="tt-bgm" id="Ending_No._02-1" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,1&#93;"><td id="" class="tt-bgm" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">BGM: Waking Up from a Waking Dream</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">BGM: 白日梦醒</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-2" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,2&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">In spite of Aimi and Kiseki's schemes in bending the rules of reality, the confrontation ended in a victory for Gensokyo's incident-resolvers.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">即便爱美和天白鹭造成了扭曲真实的异变，幻想乡的城管还是取得了最终的胜利。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-3" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,3&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Kasen could tell Aimi wasn't in the right state of mind to talk things over, so she arranged for a meeting at the Hakurei Shrine the next morning. She and Reimu would discuss the technicalities of reversing the incident with Aimi and Kiseki.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">华扇能感受到爱美现在心态爆炸，完全无法交涉，所以她选择在第二天在博丽神社组织一场会议，她将与灵梦及异变的主谋们讨论如何回溯这场异变。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-4" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,4&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Kasen also invited Nunokae to explain what happened when she met the masterminds, and Marisa and Sanae decided to attend as well.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">她还邀请了布返来讲讲遇到幕后主使后发生了什么，魔理沙和早苗也决定参加。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-5" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,5&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Having had the night to reflect, Aimi explained why she wanted to rewrite reality. Kasen's conclusion was that Aimi's motivations were more complex than "creating a better world" or "making Rikuto love her again". While she may have started with selfish intentions, she also had a genuine desire to change the world for the better.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">花了一晚上来回想发生了什么，爱美向大家解释了为什么她想重塑现实。华扇的结论是爱美的动机远不只是“为了创造一个更好的世界”还是“让陆斗重新爱她”这两种想法而已。可能她最开始的动机确实是自私的，但她最后确实想让世界变得更好的。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-6" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,6&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Since Aimi and Kiseki's combat abilities were enhanced by dream logic, they wouldn't be powerful enough to travel outside the Human Village and see Gensokyo once the world was put back to normal. Reimu and Nunokae agreed to help catch them up on spell card experience, and Reimu offered to let them visit the shrine whenever they liked. With this out of the way, the next topic was how to fix reality.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">因为爱美和天白鹭的战斗能力只是由梦逻辑拔高了，所以她们在世界恢复正常后没有强大到能走出人类村落来探索幻想乡。灵梦和布返答应帮助她们训练符卡技能，灵梦同时邀请他们随时来做客。解决了这件事之后，下一个话题就是如何修复破碎的现实。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-7" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,7&#93;"><td id="鬼人正邪" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">鬼人正邪</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Kiseki, Aimi had you create the Tree of Aspects as an illustration to keep track of all the millions of aspects of existence, right?</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"剪世树，爱美和你一起创造了相之树来监测这成千上万相的碎片对吧？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-8" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,8&#93;"><td id="天白鹭剪世树" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">天白鹭剪世树</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">That's indeed true.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"没错。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-9" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,9&#93;"><td id="鬼人正邪" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">鬼人正邪</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">So, in order to put everything back to normal, you just need to reverse all those changes. I would think that'd be a lot faster.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"所以要是想让所有都恢复正常，你只需要把那些改变反着来一遍就好了，这肯定是更快的方法。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-10" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,10&#93;"><td id="天白鹭剪世树" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">天白鹭剪世树</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">That should be the case.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"应该是这样的没错。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-11" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,11&#93;"><td id="茨木华扇" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">茨木华扇</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">You're able to get started on that right away, right, Kiseki?</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"你现在就能开始吧剪世树？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-12" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,12&#93;"><td id="天白鹭剪世树" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">天白鹭剪世树</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">I am. But I'm not comfortable beginning unless Aimi wishes it to be so.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"可以是可以，但我在得到爱美决定重做这一切的指令之前可能做不到。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-13" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,13&#93;"><td id="茨木华扇" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">茨木华扇</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">...Well, Aimi. Can you give her your approval to start reversing all the changes?</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"...那爱美，给她重做这一切变化的指示许可吧？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-14" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,14&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Aimi shifted her arms uncomfortably.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">爱美不自在地摆动着手臂。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-15" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,15&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">灯笼坂爱美</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Yeah, I guess I could tell her to do that...</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"行吧，我觉得我能告诉她来重做了..."</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-16" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,16&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Aimi still sounded worried, so Marisa did her best to sound sympathetic.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">爱美看起来仍然忧心忡忡，魔理沙尝试努力用充满同情心的语句安慰她。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-17" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,17&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Are you still disappointed that we're makin' you reverse the dream logic?</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"你还是对于我们要求你重做梦逻辑的一切而失望吗？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-18" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,18&#93;"><td id="茨木华扇" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">茨木华扇</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">I hope you can accept that we have to destroy what you built, Aimi. Gensokyo just can't hold itself together with something like dream logic controlling reality. We've all expressed our appreciation for how badly you wanted to serve Gensokyo, but we also can't allow the way you did it to continue. I know it's hard to be clear about both at the same time.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"咱希望你能理解接受我们需要毁掉你做的梦逻辑，但是爱美啊，由梦逻辑主宰的幻想乡是不能维持自己不崩溃的。我们都对你希望拯救幻想乡的想法表示认可和感谢，但我们不能让你继续异变了，我知道同时解释这两件事是很难的。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-19" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,19&#93;"><td id="茨木华扇" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">茨木华扇</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">So...let me just ask you this. Do you admit that your actions were mistaken?</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"那...我问你这个问题，你承认你的举动是错误的吗？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-20" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,20&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">灯笼坂爱美</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Well, I...I'm thinking about it like this. I had a faint inkling that there might be problems like accidentally creating a virus youkai.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"啊，我...我是这么想的，我知道我们进行异变的时候事情出错了。我也隐隐想到可能我创造了一个病毒妖怪这类的问题。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-21" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,21&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">灯笼坂爱美</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">And you guys showed me some things I hadn't even realized. But when you all came to the Tree of Aspects, I just couldn't admit it.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"你们还向我展示了很多我没想到的事情，比如多为他人想和同情并不是完全对等的，但当你们全来相之树时，我已经无法承认了。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-22" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,22&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">灯笼坂爱美</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Rikuto and the life he offered me was the embodiment of everything I wanted to have. Everything I wanted my life to be. I was in love, and I was blinded by that love. And by the desperation to make my dreams come true. I couldn't stop my emotions. I couldn't consider any possibility other than getting my wish. Until I was defeated, because then I HAD to consider other possibilities.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"陆斗和他给我的生命是我想要的一切，我想要我生命去成为的一切，我坠入了爱河并被爱情蒙蔽了双眼，我急切地想要梦想成真，我无法控制我的情绪，没有考虑任何其他的选项，直到我被击败了，不得不开始考虑其他的可能性。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-23" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,23&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">灯笼坂爱美</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">So, yes, I...I'd agree that it was a mistake. I kept mix-and-matchin' them, and I got pretty frustrated.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"但当我把它们带回家时，无论我怎么混合他们都没有新的魔法产生，当时我也很烦恼。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-45" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,45&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">I got SOME magic, sure. They just happened to grow in those specific places.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我还是搞出了一点魔法的，但不是那种我想要的新颖有趣的魔法。那些真菌和植物其实和幻想乡其他地方的没有两样。它们只是凑巧长在了那奇异地方。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-46" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,46&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">I really should've known they'd give me more of the usual, but y'know WHY I wanted somethin' new so badly?</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我也应该知道这一点的，但你知道为啥我如此希望用它们造出新魔法吗？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-47" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,47&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">灯笼坂爱美</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">How come?</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"为什么？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-48" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,48&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">'Cause I spent so long gettin' the stuff. If I accepted they weren't gonna give me new magic, I'd have to admit that long trip was pretty much for nothin'. It was hard to realize that's what I was subconsciously sayin' to myself, but after enough hours pointlessly tryin' to get magic that wasn't there, I admitted it.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"'因为我收集这些东西花了那么长时间，如果没有新魔法作为回报，我就必须承认之前的功夫差不多白费了。'，这一点时很难承认的，我无限的用这些话语无形麻痹自己，直到是了足够多次的我终于承认了这个结果。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-49" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,49&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">And ya know what I did after that?</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"你知道咱之后做了什么吗？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-50" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,50&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">灯笼坂爱美</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">What's that?</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"什么？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-51" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,51&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">I went back to my usual materials and just combined 'em in new ways like I usually do. And whaddya know, just a little while after that I figured out how to channel spirit power into a bomb that can blast away enemy danmaku. I'd been wantin' to try that for a while. We actually used a variation on that technique to create the Aspect Shifts.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我又用回了那些普通的材料，但这一次我使用了新的方法来混合它们，你猜怎么着？不一会我就发现了一个往炸弹中注入灵力就可以摧毁敌方弹幕的魔法，一直想试试。我们在相位转换中也用到了这个技巧。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-52" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,52&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">So, do you know why I told you that story?</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"所以你知道为什么我给你讲这个故事吗？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-53" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,53&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">灯笼坂爱美</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Is it because you wanted something you couldn't get, and in order to stop wasting time and energy on it, you had to admit you couldn't get it?</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"是因为你想告诉我你也曾遇到得不到的东西，所以如果遇到这种问题应该及时承认自己的问题，这样就不会浪费更多时间和精力了？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-54" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,54&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">That's right. But there's more to it than that.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"是这样的，但也不止这样。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-55" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,55&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">I understand how you feel about havin' dreams. You'd never do anythin' in life if you didn't have dreams to make ya want to do things. But on the flip side, ya can't let those wants blind you to what's really goin' on.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我明白你对梦的感情，若没有梦去指引你去做事的话，你现在也一事无成的。但相对来说，你也不能让梦蒙蔽了现实。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-56" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,56&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">When you feel those emotions, instead of lettin' them control you...what if you tried to CHANNEL 'em? If you've got such strong feelings about makin' a better world, why don't you let that be all the MORE reason to think about it logically?</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"当你有哪些情绪时，除了让它们控制你，何不尝试引导它们一下，如果你真的那么想将世界变得更好，那为什么不用更清晰的逻辑来思考呢？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-57" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,57&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">With those emotions by themselves, you might not be considering everythin', or you might even be wrong! If you really care about a better world, then if you were wrong about how to make one, you'd wanna know that, right?</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"就这些情绪本身，你可能不会考虑的完全周全，可能说不定也会跑偏，如果你真的想创建更好的世界，那当他出错的时候你肯定想知道的不是吗？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-58" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,58&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">So that's my totally effective therapeutic advice. Try to let your emotions and your logic work together instead of against each other. Well, that's just what I think, anyway.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"这就是咱的百分百有效疗法！尝试着让你的情绪和逻辑相辅相成而不是相互对抗，这就是咱的想法啦。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-59" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,59&#93;"><td id="博丽灵梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">博丽灵梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Decided to be helpful and mature for once, huh?</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"您终于长大了，能帮忙了？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-60" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,60&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">I'm just...uh...bein'...helpin'...DREAM LOGIC! If they were created by the reality-warping power of dream logic, surely Marisa would be able to unlock some magical properties from them.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">会议继续了，少女们开始讨论爱美具体需要做什么来向世界展现她的爱，但一旦开始向爱美讲故事，魔理沙的思绪就神游到了她在幻想乡发现的奇特棱镜和花朵，如果他们是由梦逻辑扭曲现实的能力造成的，那魔理沙肯定弄从其中提取出什么新的魔法特性。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-64" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,64&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">And if they were going to disappear once the dream logic was reversed, she should get started right away! Once the meeting had concluded, Marisa collected a few glass flowers and brought them back home for experimentation.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">若它们在梦逻辑反向作用后就会消失，那这研究就刻不容缓了！会议结束后魔理沙收集了一些并回去开始了她的研究。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-65" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,65&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Darn it, why isn't this producin' anything different? Y'know, I should really learn to take my own advice.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"干哦，为啥产物还是和平时一样啊，我真该听听我自己给爱美的建议才行"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-66" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,66&#93;"><td id="风见幽香" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">风见幽香</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Salutations, Marisa! Maybe the roots would have some different properties?</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"你没有试试用根部吗？这些植物也都是从土里长出来的吧，创造它们的梦逻辑一定是先影响了它们生长的土壤，可能使用根部会得到不同的结果？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-75" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,75&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Oh, shoot, I didn't even get around to tryin' that yet. Guess that makes sense. Thanks for the help.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"看起来根部可以增加能量强度，而花瓣只会影响外观...啊这有点道理的，谢啦。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-82" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,82&#93;"><td id="风见幽香" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">风见幽香</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Of course. You're lucky I still have that extra altruism from the dream logic. Instead of you having to steal my danmaku ideas, I'm just giving them to you.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"确实，你应该谢谢我因为梦逻辑而产生的利他主义善意还剩下点，我就直接把这发现拱手相让了，要不然你还要从我这里偷哎"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._02-83" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,83&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">...Oh, hush.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"...啊闭嘴啦。"<br></div></td></tr><tr class="tt-header" id="Ending_No._02-84" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,84&#93;"><td id="" class="tt-h" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Aesthetic Relativism Team's Ending: "Dream of a Logical World</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">审美相对组结局: "逻辑世界之梦"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-header" id="Ending_No._02-85" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 02&quot;,85&#93;"><td id="" class="tt-h" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Congratulations on a 1-credit clear!</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">恭喜 1-credit 通关！</div></td></tr></tbody></table>





[](./文件-东方实在相ED1_1.png.md)

ENDING No.2 插图





[^cite_note-1]: 根据音乐评论，T.N.G.的意思是“中立的少女”（The Netural Girl）。
